\DoxyCodeLine{06832\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ issue-\/440:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06833\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 'SHOULD'\ in\ glTF\ spec\ means\ 'RECOMMENDED',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06834\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ So\ there\ is\ a\ situation\ that\ Chunk1(BIN)\ is\ composed\ of\ zero-\/sized\ BIN\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06835\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (chunksize(0)\ +\ binformat(BIN)\ =\ 8bytes).}}
